 Surgical Strike-kisi bhi simit kshetra main sena jab dushmano or aatankiyon ko nuksaan pahunchane or unhen maar giraane ke liye sainya karwai karti he to use Surgical Strike kehete hai

 What you are searching for and how much information you have about it is more important that you use the right symbol or special character with the right keywords
 kuch aise tips hai jinhen apanaakar aap apane search ko aasaan banane ke saath hi tej bana sakate hai
 1) If you are looking for something about which you have a lot of information and want to get information other than that, then search for a minus (-) symbol between two keywords
 2) agar kisi shop kii lokation talash rahe hai to behatar hoga us shop ke naam ke saath sthaan kaa pin code tip kar search karen
 3) Use one word instead of multiple words
 isse sateek link tak pahunchaa ja saktaa he
 4) If you are looking for a quotation, then write quotation directly and use quotation mark ('') on both sides of it
 5) koshish karen ki agar kisi popular verde ko likh rahe hai to uske saath ek-do or kii-verde tip karen
 6) If you are looking for a content and you know the name of the website related to it, then write the name of the website using (:) after the key word
 7) agar koi khaas formet dhund rahe hai to kii-verde ke saath (:) lagaakar file tip kaa prayog karen
 For example- budget 2014: pdf or budget 2014: XLS8) If writing many words related to one topic, use (:) between them
 udhaaharan ke liye- manjhi:resign:aajtak9) agar aapke paas koi yuarel he or usase sambandhit content dhundhna chaahate hai to related: ke baad us yuarel ko tip karen
 10) If looking for an item within a price range then two dots (
 
 )
 udhaaharan ke liye- iphone INR 4 xxrep 4 0 
 
 6 xxrep 4 0 11) number ko conwart karne liye sidhe search box main tip karen
 For example- $ 500 to INR12) To know the time in any part of the world, write the name of the country giving space with time directly
 13) mausam kaa haal jaanane ke liye weather ke saath spes dekar shahar kaa naam tip karen
 14) If you are looking for definition of a term, then type that term by giving space after define:
 15) aap google par image se related image bhi search kar sakate hai
 For this, drag the save image directly into your hard disk in the search box
 16) agar aap do chizon main se kisi ek kii talash kar rahe hai to donon verde ke bich OR kaa istemaal karen
 17) If you want to find something by adding any two terms, then use & between the two terms
 jaise- kohli & world cup18) google search kaa istemaal calculator ke taur par bhi kiya ja saktaa he
 Use + - * / % for this

 1
 Oil production in the US has doubled in the last 6 years

 2

 3
 In Europe and developing countries, the use of low fuel vehicles is also being emphasized

 4

 kuch dal aise bhi honge jo gathbandhan main sidhe taur par bhale na juden, baahar se samarthan de sakate hai, jaisaa samaajawaadee party or bahujan samaaj party ne pehle kiya tha
 "congress sources say that if the upa's existing allies want to compromise with any other party at the local level, then the Congress President has given them an exemption
 ve apane rajyon main majboot dalon se samjhauta kar sakate hai

 masalan, bihar main rajd or tamilnadu main dramuk ko yah chhot di gai he

 co / CMT5TRJ9DW Actor Tiger Shroff, who plays a superhero in the film 'A Flying Jatt', says that watching Hrithik Roshan's 'krrish' has been very inspiring for him
 'heropanti' ke abhinayta ko ummid he ki vah bhi ruthik ke str ko chhu paaenge
 Tiger said, i have become a super hero in 'A Flying Jatt', hope to do justice to this character
 vaise main yah soch bhi nahin rahaa hum ki vah kar paaungaa jo ruthik roshan ne 'krish' main kiya he
 But i will do so much that the makers of this film do not have to look down
 unhone kaha, agar main ruthik roshan ke str ko chhu paaya to vaaki kamaal ho jayega
 Hrithik sir has given a wonderful film
 sirf dekhne bhar se main prerit ho gaya or ab main koshish karuunga ki jaise-taise vahaan tak pahunch jaaun
 Hrithik Roshan's fan Tiger himself is also an amazing dancer and is a fitness freak
 bilkul apane adarsh ke samaan
 The comments unhone kaha, ruthik mere adarsh hai
 i wanted to dance like Hrithik since childhood
 main unki sabhi filmein dekha karata tha or 'kaho naa pyaar he' ne to mujhe divaana bana diya tha
 Every night before bed i used to watch their videos and imagine that i am dancing in the video
 dhire-dhire maine unke body laguage ko samajha
 i have not reached there yet, but i am trying
 philhal tiger apni aane vaali film 'baagi' kii shooting puri kar rahe hai
